**Trade‑Insights Summary (as of the latest loop)**  

| **What the data tells us** | **Key take‑aways** |
|----------------------------|--------------------|
| **Overall performance** | • **0 wins, all losses** across every instrument. <br>• Total‑PnL is negative for every symbol – the worst cumulative loss is **‑0.338 USD** on **RESOLV‑USDT**; the best (least negative) is **‑0.000006 USD** on **W‑USDT**. |
| **Big‑winner‑style guidance** (the “big winners pay for small losers” rule) | • The system is currently **unable to identify any “big‑winner” candidates** – all symbols have `best_win = 0` and `avg_win = 0`. <br>• The “top symbols” list (VELVET, BOME, GUN, ZORA, PTB, W, S, AVAAI) shows **zero historic profit** and several are **blocked** (VELVET, AVAAI, POPCAT, etc.). |
| **Repeated losers** | • Symbols with **≥ 3 losses** (blocked count) should be avoided: <br>  – **AVAAI‑USDT** (3 blocks, 1 loss) <br>  – **POPCAT‑USDT** (4 blocks) <br>  – **DRIFT‑USDT** (5 blocks) <br>  – **Q‑USDT** (11 blocks) |
| **Recent activity** | • **Orders placed** (sell side, market) on: GUN, ZORA, NOM, BOME, USELESS, BTW, GWEI, etc. <br>• **Positions closed** with realized losses on: <br>  – **AVAAI‑USDT** (‑0.000038 USD) <br>  – **USELESS‑USDT** (‑0.000403 USD) <br>  – **NOM‑USDT** (‑0.000009 USD) <br>  – **GWEI‑USDT** (‑0.000719 USD) <br>  – **BTW‑USDT** (‑0.01244 USD) <br>  – **Q‑USDT** (‑0.001028 USD) <br>  – **PUMP‑USDT** (‑0.00541 USD) |
| **Risk‑/Reward‑profile** | • Current stop‑losses are hitting (average loss ≈ 0.001 USD) while **no take‑profit has ever been hit**. <br>• The system is therefore **cutting losers quickly** (as intended) but **never letting winners run** – there are simply no winners to run. |
| **Symbol‑stats highlights** | • **Highest total‑PnL (least negative)**: `W‑USDT` (‑0.000006 USD) – only 1 trade, not blocked. <br>• **Most trades**: `XAI‑USDT` (15 trades) – still all losses, heavily blocked (10). <br>• **Largest single loss**: `RESOLV‑USDT` (‑0.338 USD) – 5 losses, 0 wins. |
| **Immediate red flags** | • **No profitable symbols** – the “big‑winner” filter cannot be satisfied. <br>• **Many symbols are blocked** – the engine is repeatedly rejecting them, indicating they have hit the 3‑loss repeat‑loser rule. <br>• **Recent orders** are still being placed on symbols with zero historic win data (e.g., GUN, ZORA) – this may be inefficient. |

### What this means for the next step
1. **Pause new entries on symbols that have been blocked ≥ 3 times** (AVAAI, POPCAT, DRIFT, Q, etc.) until a fresh, high‑volume breakout appears.  
2. **Shift focus to symbols with any positive historic win** – currently none exist, so we need to **expand the candidate pool** (use `blofin_rank_opportunities` with a higher 24‑h change filter) to capture fresh movers that could become the next “big winner”.  
3. **Re‑evaluate TP/SL sizing** – the current loss‑average (~0.001 USD) is tiny; consider widening the stop‑loss to the 1‑1.2 % range (per Profit Doctrine) while keeping the TP at 5‑10 % to allow asymmetric payoff.  
4. **Logically, the system should not place orders on symbols with 0 wins and 0 avg_win** unless they have a strong 24‑h momentum signal. Adjust the entry filter to require either:  
   - `avg_win > 0` **or**  
   - `24h % change > 8 %` **and** `volume > threshold`.  

These adjustments will help the engine start finding true “big‑winner” setups rather than repeatedly taking tiny losses.
